                    7. gotoIf($["${ISNULL(${BLINDTRANSFER})}" = "1"]?asisitida:ciega) [pbx_config]
     [ciega]        8. set(CANAL=${CUT(BLINDTRANSFER,,1)})        [pbx_config]
                    9. Set(NombreExt=${CUT(CANAL,\/,2)})          [pbx_config]
                    10. Noop(${CHANNEL} -- ${CANAL} -- ${SIPPEER(${NombreExt},curcalls)} ${UNIQUEID} ${BRIDGEDUNIQUEID}) [pbx_config]
                    11. goto(inicio)                              [pbx_config]
     [asisitida]    12. set(CANAL=${CUT(TRANSFERERNAME,,1)})      [pbx_config]
                    13. Set(NombreExt=${CUT(CANAL,\/,2)})         [pbx_config]
                    14. Noop(${CHANNEL} -- ${CANAL} -- ${SIPPEER(${NombreExt},curcalls)}) [pbx_config]
                    15. goto(inicio)                              [pbx_config]
     [inicio]       16. set(TRANSFERENTE=${CUT(CANAL,\/,2)})      [pbx_config]
                    17. set(TIPO=${CUT(CANAL,\/,1)})              [pbx_config]
                    18. gotoIf($["${TIPO}" = "DAHDI"]?ANALOGA:VOIP) [pbx_config]
     [VOIP]         19. Set(CONTEXTO=${ODBC_DY_CONTEXTOS_Voip(${TRANSFERENTE})}) [pbx_config]
                    20. execIf($["${ISNULL(${CONTEXTO})}" = "1"]?Set(CONTEXTO=Agentes)) [pbx_config]
                    21. goto(${CONTEXTO},${EXTEN},1))             [pbx_config]
     [ANALOGA]      22. Set(CONTEXTO=${ODBC_DY_CONTEXTOS_Analogo(${TRANSFERENTE})}) [pbx_config]
                    23. execIf($["${ISNULL(${CONTEXTO})}" = "1"]?Set(CONTEXTO=Agentes)) [pbx_config]
                    24. goto(${CONTEXTO},${EXTEN},1))             [pbx_config]

     [next]         12. Set(I=$[${I} + 1])                        [pbx_config]

                    14. ChannelRedirect(${BRIDGEPEER},ConferenciaLlamate,${CONFNO},1) [pbx_config]
                    15. ChannelRedirect(${CHANNEL},ConferenciaExtension,${CONFNO},1) [pbx_config]

[ Context 'macro-GrabacionExt' created by 'pbx_config' ]
  'h' =>            1. macroexit()                                [pbx_config]
  's' =>            1. GotoIf($[${LEN(${BLINDTRANSFER})} > 0]?2:4) [pbx_config]
                    2. StopMixMonitor()                           [pbx_config]

     [verifica1]    13. GotoIf($["${ISNULL(${tipo_grabacion})}" = "1"]?:verifica2) [pbx_config]

     [verifica2]    15. GotoIf($["${ISNULL(${tipo_grabacion})}" = "1"]?:verifica3) [pbx_config]
                    16. Macroexit()                               [pbx_config]
     [verifica3]    17. ExecIf($[${NumExtension} >= 900 && ${NumExtension} < 999]?SET(tipo_grabacion=T)) [pbx_config]
     [inicio]       18. ExecIf($["${tipo_grabacion}"!="T"]?macroexit) [pbx_config]
     [sigue]        19. SET(calltime=${STRFTIME(${EPOCH},,%H%M%S)}) [pbx_config]

                    22. system(/bin/mkdir -p ${calldir})          [pbx_config]

                    24. Set(__userfield=${calldir}/${CALLFILENAME}.gsm) [pbx_config]
                    25. Set(SHARED(userfield,${CDR(channel)})=${userfield}) [pbx_config]
                    26. Set(CDR(userfield)=${userfield})          [pbx_config]
                    27. MixMonitor(${calldir}/${CALLFILENAME}.gsm) [pbx_config]
                    28. macroexit()                               [pbx_config]

[ Context 'SubResultadoLlamadaExterna' created by 'pbx_config' ]

[ Context 'SubResultadoLlamada' created by 'pbx_config' ]
  's-ANSWER' =>     1. NoOp(Llamada contestada)                   [pbx_config]
                    2. Return("OK")                               [pbx_config]
  's-BUSY' =>       1. Set(i=1)                                   [pbx_config]
                    2. SET(Extension=none)                        [pbx_config]
                    3. SET(Extensiones=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[rotacion])}) [pbx_config]
                    4. noop(${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})} ${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[rotacion])}) [pbx_config]
                    5. While($[${ISNULL(${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})}!=1]) [pbx_config]
                    6. ExecIf($["${DEVICE_STATE(SIP/${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})}"="NOT_INUSE"]?SET(Extension=${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})) [pbx_config]
                    7. ExecIf($["${DEVICE_STATE(SIP/${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})}"="NOT_INUSE"]?goto(s-NOANSWER,okext)) [pbx_config]
                    8. Set(i=$[${i} + 1])                         [pbx_config]
                    9. EndWhile()                                 [pbx_config]
     [okext]        10. ExecIf($["${Extension}"!="none"]?goto(Extensiones,${Extension},1)) [pbx_config]
                    11. SET(BUZON_VOZ=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[BUZON_VOZ])}) [pbx_config]
                    12. SET(mailbox_conf=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[mailbox_conf])}) [pbx_config]
                    13. SET(context=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},context)}) [pbx_config]
                    14. SET(desborde=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[DESBORDE])}) [pbx_config]
                    15. SET(numero_externo=${CUT(desborde,\,,2)}) [pbx_config]
                    16. ExecIf($["${TipoExtension}"=="DAHDI"]?Set(ARRAY(mailbox,mailbox_conf,desborde,numero_externo,context)=${ODBC_DY_DESBORDES_EXTENSION(${ARG1})})) [pbx_config]
                    17. Gotoif($["${BUZON_VOZ}"=="1"]?:verificaDesborde) [pbx_config]
                    18. VoiceMail(${mailbox_conf},b)              [pbx_config]
                    19. hangup(16)                                [pbx_config]
     [verificaDesborde] 20. Gotoif($["${desborde}"!="0"]?:retorno)    [pbx_config]
                    21. Set(ARRAY(mailbox_conf,BUZON_VOZ,desborde,numero_externo,es_analoga,canal_analogo,email,context)=${ODBC_DY_DESBORDES_EXTENSION(${ARG1})}) [pbx_config]
                    22. System(/var/lib/asterisk/agi-bin/EnvioCorreo.agi ${email} ${STRFTIME(${EPOCH},,%Y-%m-%d_%H:%M:%S)} ${CALLERID(name)} ${CALLERID(num)} &) [pbx_config]
                    23. goto(${context},${numero_externo},1)      [pbx_config]
                    24. hangup(16)                                [pbx_config]
     [retorno]      25. Playback(silence/1,noanswer)              [pbx_config]
                    26. Return("OK")                              [pbx_config]
  's-CANCEL' =>     1. Playback(silence/1,noanswer)               [pbx_config]
                    2. Return("OK")                               [pbx_config]
  's-CHANUNAVAIL' => 1. Set(i=1)                                   [pbx_config]
                    2. SET(Extension=none)                        [pbx_config]
                    3. SET(Extensiones=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[rotacion])}) [pbx_config]
                    4. noop(${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})} ${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[rotacion])}) [pbx_config]
                    5. While($[${ISNULL(${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})}!=1]) [pbx_config]
                    6. ExecIf($["${DEVICE_STATE(SIP/${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})}"="NOT_INUSE"]?SET(Extension=${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})) [pbx_config]
                    7. ExecIf($["${DEVICE_STATE(SIP/${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})}"="NOT_INUSE"]?goto(s-NOANSWER,okext)) [pbx_config]
                    8. Set(i=$[${i} + 1])                         [pbx_config]
                    9. EndWhile()                                 [pbx_config]
     [okext]        10. ExecIf($["${Extension}"!="none"]?goto(Extensiones,${Extension},1)) [pbx_config]
                    11. SET(BUZON_VOZ=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[BUZON_VOZ])}) [pbx_config]
                    12. SET(mailbox_conf=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[mailbox_conf])}) [pbx_config]
                    13. SET(context=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},context)}) [pbx_config]
                    14. SET(desborde=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[DESBORDE])}) [pbx_config]
                    15. SET(numero_externo=${CUT(desborde,\,,2)}) [pbx_config]
                    16. ExecIf($["${TipoExtension}"=="DAHDI"]?Set(ARRAY(mailbox_conf,BUZON_VOZ,desborde,numero_externo,es_analoga,canal_analogo,email,context)=${ODBC_DY_DESBORDES_EXTENSION(${ARG1})})) [pbx_config]
                    17. Gotoif($["${BUZON_VOZ}"=="1"]?:verificaDesborde) [pbx_config]
                    18. VoiceMail(${mailbox_conf},u)              [pbx_config]
                    19. hangup(16)                                [pbx_config]
     [verificaDesborde] 20. Gotoif($["${desborde}"!="0"]?:retorno)    [pbx_config]
                    21. Set(ARRAY(mailbox_conf,BUZON_VOZ,desborde,numero_externo,es_analoga,canal_analogo,email,context)=${ODBC_DY_DESBORDES_EXTENSION(${ARG1})}) [pbx_config]
                    22. System(/var/lib/asterisk/agi-bin/EnvioCorreo.agi ${email} ${STRFTIME(${EPOCH},,%Y-%m-%d_%H:%M:%S)} ${CALLERID(name)} ${CALLERID(num)} &) [pbx_config]
                    23. goto(${context},${numero_externo},1)      [pbx_config]
                    24. hangup(16)                                [pbx_config]
     [retorno]      25. Playback(silence/1,noanswer)              [pbx_config]
                    26. Return("OK")                              [pbx_config]
  's-CONGESTION' => 1. Playback(silence/1,noanswer)               [pbx_config]
                    2. Return("OK")                               [pbx_config]
  's-NOANSWER' =>   1. Set(i=1)                                   [pbx_config]
                    2. SET(Extension=none)                        [pbx_config]
                    3. SET(Extensiones=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[rotacion])}) [pbx_config]
                    4. noop(${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})} ${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[rotacion])}) [pbx_config]
                    5. While($[${ISNULL(${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})}!=1]) [pbx_config]
                    6. ExecIf($["${DEVICE_STATE(SIP/${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})}"="NOT_INUSE"]?SET(Extension=${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})) [pbx_config]
                    7. ExecIf($["${DEVICE_STATE(SIP/${CUT(Extensiones,,${i})})}"="NOT_INUSE"]?goto(s-NOANSWER,okext)) [pbx_config]
                    8. Set(i=$[${i} + 1])                         [pbx_config]
                    9. EndWhile()                                 [pbx_config]
     [okext]        10. ExecIf($["${Extension}"!="none"]?goto(Extensiones,${Extension},1)) [pbx_config]
                    11. SET(BUZON_VOZ=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[BUZON_VOZ])}) [pbx_config]
                    12. SET(mailbox_conf=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[mailbox_conf])}) [pbx_config]
                    13. SET(context=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},context)}) [pbx_config]
                    14. SET(desborde=${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},chanvar[DESBORDE])}) [pbx_config]
                    15. SET(numero_externo=${CUT(desborde,\,,2)}) [pbx_config]
                    16. ExecIf($["${TipoExtension}"=="DAHDI"]?Set(ARRAY(mailbox,mailbox_conf,desborde,numero_externo,context)=${ODBC_DY_DESBORDES_EXTENSION(${ARG1})})) [pbx_config]
                    17. Gotoif($["${BUZON_VOZ}"=="1"]?:verificaDesborde) [pbx_config]
                    18. VoiceMail(${mailbox_conf},u)              [pbx_config]
                    19. hangup(16)                                [pbx_config]
     [verificaDesborde] 20. Gotoif($["${desborde}"!="0"]?:retorno)    [pbx_config]
                    21. Set(ARRAY(mailbox_conf,BUZON_VOZ,desborde,numero_externo,es_analoga,canal_analogo,email,context)=${ODBC_DY_DESBORDES_EXTENSION(${ARG1})}) [pbx_config]
                    22. System(/var/lib/asterisk/agi-bin/EnvioCorreo.agi ${email} ${STRFTIME(${EPOCH},,%Y-%m-%d_%H:%M:%S)} ${CALLERID(name)} ${CALLERID(num)} &) [pbx_config]
                    23. goto(${context},${numero_externo},1)      [pbx_config]
                    24. hangup(16)                                [pbx_config]
     [retorno]      25. Playback(silence/1,noanswer)              [pbx_config]
                    26. Return("OK")                              [pbx_config]
  '_s-.' =>         1. Playback(silence/1,noanswer)               [pbx_config]
                    2. Return("OK")                               [pbx_config]

[ Context 'SubValidaClaveSalidaLLamadas' created by 'pbx_config' ]
  's' =>            1. Gotoif($["${SIPPEER(${NumExtension},context)}"="Agentes"]?perfilNoPermitido:validaClave) [pbx_config]
     [perfilNoPermitido] 2. Playback(DyPerfilNoPermitido)              [pbx_config]
                    3. Goto(retornaFalso)                         [pbx_config]
     [validaClave]  4. Gotoif($["${DY_PIDE_CLAVE}"="1"]?autenticacion:validaClavePreIngresada) [pbx_config]
     [autenticacion] 5. Read(CLAVE_DIGITADA,DyDigiteClave,4,,2,3)  [pbx_config]
                    6. Set(AGPASS=${DB(dy_cbx_agentes_claves/${CLAVE_DIGITADA})}) [pbx_config]
                    7. ExecIf($["${ISNULL(${AGPASS})}"!="1"]?SET(DY_AGI_CLAVE_VALIDA_T=SI):SET(DY_AGI_CLAVE_VALIDA_T=NO)) [pbx_config]
     [validaClavePreIngresada] 8. GotoIf($["${DY_AGI_CLAVE_VALIDA_T}"="SI"]?retornaVerdadero:claveNoValida) [pbx_config]
     [retornaVerdadero] 9. Return("CLAVE_OK")                         [pbx_config]
     [claveNoValida] 10. Playback(DyClaveNoValida)                 [pbx_config]
     [retornaFalso] 11. Return("FALLO")                           [pbx_config]

[ Context 'macro-MarcadoH323' created by 'pbx_config' ]
  's' =>            1. Set(_NumExtension=${CALLERID(num)})        [pbx_config]
                    2. Set(_NumTelefono=${ARG1})                  [pbx_config]
                    3. Set(_DY_NUMERO=${ARG1})                    [pbx_config]
                    4. Set(DY_TRONCAL=${ARG2})                    [pbx_config]
                    5. Set(DY_DURACION_TIMBRE=${ARG3})            [pbx_config]
                    6. Set(DY_OPCIONES=${ARG4}))                  [pbx_config]
                    7. Set(DY_PIDE_CLAVE=${ARG5})                 [pbx_config]
                    8. Set(DY_NUMERO_ANTEPUESTO=${ARG6})          [pbx_config]

                    10. GoSub(SubValidaClaveSalidaLLamadas,s,1(${NumExtension},${DY_NUMERO:-4},${DY_NUMERO})) [pbx_config]
                    11. NoOp(RESULTADO SUBRUTINA ${GOSUB_RETVAL}) [pbx_config]
                    12. GotoIf($[${GOSUB_RETVAL}="CLAVE_OK"]?marcar:salida) [pbx_config]
     [marcar]       13. AGI(h323ip.agi,${DY_TRONCAL})             [pbx_config]
                    14. Dial(OOH323/${DY_NUMERO_ANTEPUESTO}${DY_NUMERO}@${IPTrl}:1720,${DY_DURACION_TIMBRE},${DY_OPCIONES}M(GrabacionExt^${OrgUniqueId}^${NumTelefono}^${NumExtension})) [pbx_config]

     [salida]       16. MacroExit()                               [pbx_config]

                    14. MacroExit()                               [pbx_config]
     [marcacionSIP] 15. Noop(tipo extension sip)                  [pbx_config]
                    16. Macro(GrabacionExt,${OrgUniqueId},${NumTelefono},${NumExtension}) [pbx_config]
